    <link rel="stylesheet" href="bootstrap/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="app.css" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="IISLogViewer.styles.css" />
    <link id="app-theme" rel="stylesheet" href="_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-default/all.css" />
    <link rel="icon" type="image/png" href="favicon.png" />
    <HeadOutlet />
</head>

    <Routes @rendermode="InteractiveServer" />
    <script src="_framework/blazor.web.js"></script>
    <script src="_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/js/telerik-blazor.js"></script>
    <script>
        window.themeSwitcher = {
            setTheme: function (themeHref) {
                var link = document.getElementById("app-theme");
                var isBootstrapTheme = !!themeHref && themeHref.indexOf("kendo-theme-bootstrap") !== -1;
                if (link) {
                    link.href = themeHref;
                    localStorage.setItem("theme", themeHref);
                }

                if (document && document.body) {
                    document.body.classList.toggle("theme-bootstrap", isBootstrapTheme);
                }
            },
            getTheme: function () {
                return localStorage.getItem("theme");
            }
        };
    </script>
</body>

</html>

@code {
    public class ThemeOption
    {
        public string Text { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Value { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private string SelectedTheme = "_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-default/all.css";

    private readonly List<ThemeOption> Themes = new()
    {
        new ThemeOption { Text = "Default", Value = "_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-default/all.css" },
        new ThemeOption { Text = "Bootstrap", Value = "_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-bootstrap/all.css" },
        new ThemeOption { Text = "Material", Value = "_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-material/all.css" },
        new ThemeOption { Text = "Fluent", Value = "_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-fluent/all.css" }
    };

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        if (firstRender)
        {
            var theme = await JS.InvokeAsync<string>("themeSwitcher.getTheme");

            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(theme))
            {
                SelectedTheme = Themes.Any(t => string.Equals(t.Value, theme, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                    ? theme
                    : "_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-default/all.css";
                await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
            }
        }

        // Re-apply the currently selected theme after renders so tab switches
        // or component refreshes cannot visually reset the active stylesheet.
        await JS.InvokeVoidAsync("themeSwitcher.setTheme", SelectedTheme);
    }

    private async Task OnThemeChanged(string value)
    {
        SelectedTheme = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value)
            ? "_content/Telerik.UI.for.Blazor/css/kendo-theme-default/all.css"
            : value;

        await JS.InvokeVoidAsync("themeSwitcher.setTheme", SelectedTheme);
    }
}

@rendermode InteractiveServer
@inject IISLogViewer.Services.LogParserService LogParser
@inject IISLogViewer.Services.SelectionState SelectionState
@inject NavigationManager NavigationManager

<div class="nav-tree">
    <nav class="nav-tree__links">
        <NavLink href="/" Match="NavLinkMatch.All" class="nav-tree__link">Dashboard</NavLink>
        <NavLink href="/report" class="nav-tree__link">View Report</NavLink>
    </nav>

    <div class="nav-tree__section">
        <div class="nav-tree__caption">Service</div>
        <div class="folder-picker">
            <TelerikTextBox Value="@_folderFilter"
                            ValueChanged="@(value => _folderFilter = value)"
                            Placeholder="Filter folders"
                            Width="100%"
                            ShowClearButton="true"
                            FillMode="@ThemeConstants.TextBox.FillMode.Outline"
                            Size="@ThemeConstants.TextBox.Size.Small" />
            <TelerikDropDownList Data="@FilteredFolders"
                                 Value="@SelectedFolder"
                                 ValueChanged="@( (string value) => OnFolderChanged(value) )"
                                 Width="100%"
                                 Filterable="true"
                                 FilterOperator="@StringFilterOperator.Contains"
                                 Size="@ThemeConstants.DropDownList.Size.Small"
                                 FillMode="@ThemeConstants.DropDownList.FillMode.Outline">
                <ItemTemplate Context="folder">
                    @LogParser.GetFolderDisplayName(folder.ToString() ?? string.Empty)
                </ItemTemplate>
            </TelerikDropDownList>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="nav-tree__caption">Log Files</div>

    @foreach (var year in LogTree.Keys.OrderByDescending(y => y))
    {
        var yearExpanded = ExpandedYears.Contains(year);
        var yearChecked = IsYearChecked(year);

        <!-- Year Row -->
        <div class="tree-row tree-year @(yearExpanded ? "expanded" : "")">
            <TelerikCheckBox Value="@yearChecked"
                             ValueChanged="@((bool value) => ToggleYear(year, value))"
                             Class="tree-checkbox" />
            <span class="tree-label" @onclick="@(() => ToggleYearExpand(year))">
                <span class="tree-arrow">@(yearExpanded ? "▾" : "▸")</span>
                <span class="tree-icon-year">Y</span>
                <strong>@year</strong>
                <TelerikChip Size="@ThemeConstants.Chip.Size.Small" Class="tree-badge">
                    @LogTree[year].Values.SelectMany(d => d).Count()
                </TelerikChip>
            </span>
        </div>

        @if (yearExpanded)
        {
            @foreach (var month in LogTree[year].Keys.OrderByDescending(m => m))
            {
                var monthKey = $"{year}-{month}";
                var monthExpanded = ExpandedMonths.Contains(monthKey);
                var monthChecked = IsMonthChecked(year, month);
                var dayCount = LogTree[year][month].Count;

                <!-- Month Row -->
                <div class="tree-row tree-month @(monthExpanded ? "expanded" : "")">
                    <TelerikCheckBox Value="@monthChecked"
                                     ValueChanged="@((bool value) => ToggleMonth(year, month, value))"
                                     Class="tree-checkbox" />
                    <span class="tree-label" @onclick="@(() => ToggleMonthExpand(year, month))">
                        <span class="tree-arrow">@(monthExpanded ? "▾" : "▸")</span>
                        <span class="tree-icon-month">M</span>
                        @GetMonthName(month)
                        <span class="day-badge">@dayCount</span>
                    </span>
                </div>

                @if (monthExpanded)
                {
                    @foreach (var day in LogTree[year][month].OrderByDescending(d => d))
                    {
                        var dayChecked = SelectedDays.Contains(day);
                        var isWeekend = day.DayOfWeek is DayOfWeek.Saturday or DayOfWeek.Sunday;
                        var holidayIcon = GetHolidayIcon(day);

                        <!-- Day Row -->
                        <div class="tree-row tree-day @(dayChecked ? "day-selected" : "") @(isWeekend ? "tree-day-weekend" : "")">
                            <TelerikCheckBox Value="@dayChecked"
                                             ValueChanged="@((bool value) => ToggleDay(day, value))"
                                             Class="tree-checkbox" />
                            <span class="tree-label tree-label-day">
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(holidayIcon))
                                {
                                    <span class="tree-icon-day">@holidayIcon</span>
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    <span class="tree-icon-day">D</span>
                                }
                                @day.ToString("ddd, dd MMM yyyy")
                            </span>
                        </div>
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
</div>

@if (SelectedDays.Any())
{
    <div class="selection-summary">
        <span class="selection-summary__status"></span>
        <span><b>@SelectedDays.Count</b> day(s) selected</span>
        <TelerikButton OnClick="@ClearAll"
                       Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small"
                       FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Flat"
                       ThemeColor="@ThemeConstants.Button.ThemeColor.Primary">
            Clear
        </TelerikButton>
    </div>
}

@code {
    private Dictionary<int, Dictionary<int, List<DateTime>>> LogTree = new();
    private HashSet<DateTime> SelectedDays = new();
    private HashSet<int> ExpandedYears = new();
    private HashSet<string> ExpandedMonths = new();

    private List<string> AvailableFolders = new();
    private string SelectedFolder = "";
    private string _folderFilter = "";

    private IEnumerable<string> FilteredFolders =>
        string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_folderFilter)
            ? AvailableFolders
            : AvailableFolders.Where(f =>
                LogParser.GetFolderDisplayName(f).Contains(_folderFilter, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                f.Contains(_folderFilter, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        AvailableFolders = LogParser.GetAvailableFolders();
        SelectedFolder = LogParser.CurrentFolder;
        LogTree = LogParser.GetLogTree();
    }

    private void OnFolderChanged(string folder)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(folder))
            return;

        SelectedFolder = folder;
        SelectedDays.Clear();
        LogParser.SetFolder(folder);
        LogTree = LogParser.GetLogTree();
        SelectionState.SelectedDays = new HashSet<DateTime>();
        SelectionState.CurrentFolder = folder;
        SelectionState.NotifyFolderChanged();
        StateHasChanged();
    }


    private string GetMonthName(int month) =>
        new DateTime(2000, month, 1).ToString("MMMM");

    private static string? GetHolidayIcon(DateTime day)
    {
        // Fixed-date holidays
        if (day.Month == 1 && day.Day == 1) return "🎆";   // New Year's Day
        if (day.Month == 2 && day.Day == 14) return "💘";  // Valentine's Day
        if (day.Month == 3 && day.Day == 17) return "☘️";  // St. Patrick's Day
        if (day.Month == 7 && day.Day == 4) return "🇺🇸";   // Independence Day
        if (day.Month == 10 && day.Day == 31) return "🎃"; // Halloween
        if (day.Month == 12 && day.Day == 25) return "🎄"; // Christmas

        // Floating US holidays
        if (IsMemorialDay(day)) return "🪖";
        if (IsThanksgiving(day)) return "🦃";

        return null;
    }

    private static bool IsMemorialDay(DateTime day)
    {
        // Last Monday in May
        return day.Month == 5 && day.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Monday && day.AddDays(7).Month != 5;
    }

    private static bool IsThanksgiving(DateTime day)
    {
        // Fourth Thursday in November
        return day.Month == 11 && day.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Thursday && day.Day >= 22 && day.Day <= 28;
    }

    private void ToggleYearExpand(int year)
    {
        if (ExpandedYears.Contains(year)) ExpandedYears.Remove(year);
        else ExpandedYears.Add(year);
    }

    private void ToggleMonthExpand(int year, int month)
    {
        var key = $"{year}-{month}";
        if (ExpandedMonths.Contains(key)) ExpandedMonths.Remove(key);
        else ExpandedMonths.Add(key);
    }

    private bool IsYearChecked(int year) =>
        LogTree[year].Values.SelectMany(d => d).All(d => SelectedDays.Contains(d));

    private bool IsMonthChecked(int year, int month) =>
        LogTree[year][month].All(d => SelectedDays.Contains(d));

    private void ToggleYear(int year, bool value)
    {
        foreach (var month in LogTree[year].Keys)
            foreach (var day in LogTree[year][month])
            {
                if (value) SelectedDays.Add(day);
                else SelectedDays.Remove(day);
            }
        NotifySelection();
    }

    private void ToggleMonth(int year, int month, bool value)
    {
        foreach (var day in LogTree[year][month])
        {
            if (value) SelectedDays.Add(day);
            else SelectedDays.Remove(day);
        }
        NotifySelection();
    }

    private void ToggleDay(DateTime day, bool value)
    {
        if (value) SelectedDays.Add(day);
        else SelectedDays.Remove(day);
        NotifySelection();
    }

    private void ClearAll()
    {
        SelectedDays.Clear();
        NotifySelection();
    }

    private void NotifySelection()
    {
        SelectionState.SelectedDays = new HashSet<DateTime>(SelectedDays);
        SelectionState.NotifyChanged();
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo("/report");
    }
}

@page "/"
@rendermode InteractiveServer
@inject IISLogViewer.Services.LogParserService LogParser

    <div>

    </div>

@if (IsLoading)
{
    <div class="loading-panel" role="status" aria-live="polite" aria-busy="true">
        <TelerikLoader Size="@ThemeConstants.Loader.Size.Large" Type="@LoaderType.InfiniteSpinner" />

    </div>

else if (OverallReport != null)
{
    <div class="stats-grid">
        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value">@OverallReport.TotalHits.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Total Hits</div>
        </article>

        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value stat-card__value--success">@SuccessCount.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Successful (2xx/3xx)</div>
        </article>

        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value stat-card__value--warning">@ClientErrorCount.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Client Errors (4xx)</div>
        </article>

        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value stat-card__value--error">@ServerErrorCount.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Server Errors (5xx)</div>

    </div>

        <Report ReportData="OverallReport" />
    </section>

else

    <div class="loading-state">No report data was found.</div>

<style>
    .page-header h1 {
        margin: 0;
        font-size: 1.45rem;
        font-weight: 700;
    }

    .page-header p {
        margin: 0.2rem 0 0.75rem;
        color: var(--kendo-color-subtle, #666);
        font-size: 0.98rem;
    }

    .stats-grid {
        display: grid;
        grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(180px, 1fr));
        gap: 0.65rem;
        margin-bottom: 0.65rem;
    }

    .stat-card {
        /* padding: 0.75rem 0.8rem; */
        border: 1px solid var(--kendo-color-border, #d4d4d4);
        border-radius: 80px;
        background: var(--kendo-color-surface, #fff);
        text-align: center;
    }

    .stat-card__value {
        font-size: 1.55rem;
        font-weight: 700;
        color: var(--kendo-color-primary, #0d6efd);
    }

    .stat-card__value--success { color: #28a745; }
    .stat-card__value--warning { color: #ff9800; }
    .stat-card__value--error { color: #f44336; }

    .stat-card__label {
        margin-top: 0.2rem;
        color: var(--kendo-color-subtle, #666);
        font-size: 0.92rem;
    }

    .surface-panel {
        border: 1px solid var(--kendo-color-border, #d4d4d4);
        border-radius: 12px;
        padding: 0.75rem;
        background: var(--kendo-color-surface, #fff);
    }

    .loading-state {
        padding: 2rem 0;
        color: var(--shell-subtle);
    }

    .loading-panel {
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        align-items: center;
        justify-content: center;
        gap: 0.75rem;
        min-height: 220px;
        border: 1px solid var(--shell-border);
        border-radius: 18px;
        background: var(--shell-panel);
    }

    .loading-panel__text {
        color: var(--shell-subtle);
        font-weight: 600;
    }
</style>

@code {
    private IISLogViewer.Services.LogReport? OverallReport;
    private int SuccessCount;
    private int ClientErrorCount;
    private int ServerErrorCount;
    private int TotalFiles;
    private int TotalYears;
    private string DateRange = "";
    private bool IsLoading = true;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            await Task.Run(() =>
            {
                var tree = LogParser.GetLogTree();
                TotalYears = tree.Count;
                TotalFiles = tree.Values.SelectMany(m => m.Values).SelectMany(d => d).Count();

                var allDates = tree.Values.SelectMany(m => m.Values).SelectMany(d => d).OrderBy(d => d).ToList();
                if (allDates.Any())
                    DateRange = $"{allDates.First():dd MMM yyyy} — {allDates.Last():dd MMM yyyy}";
            });

            // Await the parse call outside the Task.Run so Blazor handles the async context naturally
            OverallReport = await LogParser.ParseAll();

            if (OverallReport != null)
            {
                SuccessCount = OverallReport.StatusCodes
                    .Where(s => s.Key >= 200 && s.Key < 400)
                    .Sum(s => s.Value);

                ClientErrorCount = OverallReport.StatusCodes
                    .Where(s => s.Key >= 400 && s.Key < 500)
                    .Sum(s => s.Value);

                ServerErrorCount = OverallReport.StatusCodes
                    .Where(s => s.Key >= 500)
                    .Sum(s => s.Value);
            }
        }
        finally
        {
            IsLoading = false;
        }
    }
}

FILE: Components/Pages/Error.razor
------------------------------------------------------------
﻿@page "/Error"
@using System.Diagnostics

<PageTitle>Error</PageTitle>

<h1 class="text-danger">Error.</h1>
<h2 class="text-danger">An error occurred while processing your request.</h2>

@if (ShowRequestId)
{
    <p>
        <strong>Request ID:</strong> <code>@RequestId</code>
    </p>
}

<h3>Development Mode</h3>
<p>
    Swapping to <strong>Development</strong> environment will display more detailed information about the error that occurred.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>The Development environment shouldn't be enabled for deployed applications.</strong>
    It can result in displaying sensitive information from exceptions to end users.
    For local debugging, enable the <strong>Development</strong> environment by setting the <strong>ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT</strong> environment variable to <strong>Development</strong>
    and restarting the app.
</p>

@code{
    [CascadingParameter]
    private HttpContext? HttpContext { get; set; }

    private string? RequestId { get; set; }
    private bool ShowRequestId => !string.IsNullOrEmpty(RequestId);

    protected override void OnInitialized() =>
        RequestId = Activity.Current?.Id ?? HttpContext?.TraceIdentifier;
}

                                <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ToggleHourSort(nameof(HourRow.HitsLabel))" FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Flat" Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small">Hits @SortGlyph(_hourSortField, _hourSortDesc, nameof(HourRow.HitsLabel))</TelerikButton>
                            </HeaderTemplate>
                            <Template Context="itemObj">
                                @{ var row = (HourRow)itemObj; }
                                <div class="text-start">@row.HitsLabel</div>
                            </Template>
                        </GridColumn>
                    </GridColumns>
                </TelerikGrid>

            }

            <HourlyHitsDetailPopup IsOpen="@_showHourlyDetailsPopup"
                                   SelectedHour="@_selectedHour"
                                   ReportData="@ReportData"
                                   OnClose="CloseHourlyPopup" />
        }
        else if (ActiveTab == TabName.Weekdays)
        {
            <div class="grid-toolbar">
                <div><h3>Day Of Week</h3></div>
            </div>

            <TelerikGrid Data="@WeekdayRows" Pageable="true" @bind-PageSize="_pageSize" Sortable="false" Size="@ThemeConstants.Grid.Size.Small">
                <GridColumns>
                    <GridColumn Field="@nameof(WeekdayListRow.DayLabel)" Title="Day">
                        <Template Context="itemObj">
                            @{ var row = (WeekdayListRow)itemObj; }
                            <a href="#"
                               class="weekday-link"
                               @onclick:preventDefault="true"
                               @onclick="() => OpenWeekdayPopup(row.DayIndex)">
                                @row.DayLabel
                            </a>
                        </Template>
                    </GridColumn>
                    <GridColumn Field="@nameof(WeekdayListRow.HitsLabel)" Title="Hits" Width="140px">
                        <Template Context="itemObj">
                            @{ var row = (WeekdayListRow)itemObj; }
                            <div class="text-start">@row.HitsLabel</div>
                        </Template>
                    </GridColumn>
                </GridColumns>
            </TelerikGrid>

            <WeekdayDetailPopup IsOpen="@_showWeekdayDetailsPopup"
                                SelectedWeekday="@_selectedWeekday"
                                ReportData="@ReportData"
                                OnClose="CloseWeekdayPopup" />
        }
        else if (ActiveTab == TabName.Users)
        {
            <div class="grid-toolbar">
                <div><h3>Users</h3></div>
                  <TelerikTextBox Value="@_searchUsers"
                            ValueChanged="OnUsersSearchChanged"
                            Placeholder="Search users"
                            Width="260px"
                            Size="@ThemeConstants.TextBox.Size.Small"
                            FillMode="@ThemeConstants.TextBox.FillMode.Outline"
                            DebounceDelay="250"
                            ShowClearButton="true" />
            </div>

            @if (!FilteredUserRows.Any())
            {
                <div class="empty-state">No user data found. Enable cs-username in IIS log fields.</div>
            }
            else
            {
                <TelerikGrid Data="@SortedUsers"
                             Pageable="true"
                             @bind-PageSize="_pageSize"
                             Sortable="false"
                             Size="@ThemeConstants.Grid.Size.Small">
                    <GridColumns>
                        <GridColumn Field="@nameof(UserRow.DisplayName)">
                            <HeaderTemplate>
                                <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ToggleUserSort(nameof(UserRow.DisplayName))" FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Flat" Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small">Name @SortGlyph(_userSortField, _userSortDesc, nameof(UserRow.DisplayName))</TelerikButton>
                            </HeaderTemplate>
                            <Template Context="itemObj">
                                @{ var row = (UserRow)itemObj; }
                                <a href="#"
                                   class="user-link"
                                   @onclick:preventDefault="true"
                                   @onclick="() => OpenUserPopup(row.UserName)">
                                    @row.DisplayName
                                </a>
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(row.Email))
                                {
                                    <div class="toolbar-subtle">@row.Email</div>
                                }
                            </Template>
                        </GridColumn>
                        <GridColumn Field="@nameof(UserRow.Department)" Width="180px">
                            <HeaderTemplate>
                                <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ToggleUserSort(nameof(UserRow.Department))" FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Flat" Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small">Department @SortGlyph(_userSortField, _userSortDesc, nameof(UserRow.Department))</TelerikButton>
                            </HeaderTemplate>
                        </GridColumn>
                        <GridColumn Field="@nameof(UserRow.HitsLabel)" Width="140px">
                            <HeaderTemplate>
                                <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ToggleUserSort(nameof(UserRow.HitsLabel))" FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Flat" Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small">Hits @SortGlyph(_userSortField, _userSortDesc, nameof(UserRow.HitsLabel))</TelerikButton>
                            </HeaderTemplate>
                            <Template Context="itemObj">
                                @{ var row = (UserRow)itemObj; }
                                <div class="text-start">@row.HitsLabel</div>
                            </Template>
                        </GridColumn>
                    </GridColumns>
                </TelerikGrid>

            }

            <UserHitsDetailPopup IsOpen="@_showUserDetailsPopup"
                                 SelectedUser="@_selectedUser"
                                 SelectedUserDisplayName="@_selectedUserDisplayName"
                                 SelectedDays="@SelectedDays"
                                 ReportData="@ReportData"
                                 OnClose="CloseUserPopup" />
        }
    </div>
</div>

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public IISLogViewer.Services.LogReport? ReportData { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public IEnumerable<DateTime>? SelectedDays { get; set; }

    private enum TabName
    {
        Pages,
        IPs,
        Errors,
        Documents,
        Popups,
        StatusCodes,
        SlowPages,
        HourlyHits,
        Weekdays,
        Users
    }

    private static readonly IReadOnlyList<TabName> Tabs = new[]
    {
        TabName.Pages,
        TabName.Documents,
        TabName.Popups,
        TabName.Users,
        TabName.HourlyHits,
        TabName.Weekdays,
        TabName.StatusCodes,
        TabName.IPs,
        TabName.Errors,
        TabName.SlowPages,
    };

    private int _activeTabIndex;

    private int ActiveTabIndex
    {
        get => _activeTabIndex;
        set
        {
            if (_activeTabIndex == value)
                return;

            _activeTabIndex = value;
            CloseAllPopups();
        }
    }

    private TabName ActiveTab =>
        ActiveTabIndex >= 0 && ActiveTabIndex < Tabs.Count ? Tabs[ActiveTabIndex] : TabName.Pages;

    private string GetTabTitle(TabName tab)
    {
        var (name, count) = tab switch
        {
            TabName.Pages => ("🔥 Pages", ReportData?.PageHits?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.IPs => ("🌐 IPs", ReportData?.TopIPs?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.Errors => ("❌ Errors", ReportData?.ErrorPages?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.Documents => ("📄 Documents", ReportData?.DocumentHits?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.Popups => ("🪟 Popups", ReportData?.PopupHits?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.StatusCodes => ("📊 Status Codes", ReportData?.StatusCodes?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.SlowPages => ("🐢 Slow Pages", ReportData?.SlowPages?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.HourlyHits => ("⏰ Hourly Hits", ReportData?.HourlyHits?.Count ?? 0),
            TabName.Weekdays => ("📅 Day Of Week", 7),
            TabName.Users => ("👤 Users", ReportData?.UserHits?.Count ?? 0),
            _ => (tab.ToString(), 0)
        };

        return $"{name} ({count:N0})";
    }

    // Search strings for each distinct tab
    private string _searchPages = "";
    private string _searchIPs = "";
    private string _searchErrors = "";
    private string _searchDocs = "";
    private string _searchPopups = "";
    private string _searchStatus = "";
    private string _searchSlow = "";
    private string _searchHours = "";
    private string _searchUsers = "";

    private IEnumerable<TopPageInsightRow> FilteredTopPageRows =>
        BuildTopPageInsights()
            .Where(row => FilterCore($"{row.Page} {row.TopNextPage}", _searchPages));

    private IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> FilteredIpRows => FilterLabelValueRows(ReportData?.TopIPs, _searchIPs);
    private IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> FilteredErrorRows => FilterLabelValueRows(ReportData?.ErrorPages, _searchErrors);
    private IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> FilteredPopupRows => FilterLabelValueRows(ReportData?.PopupHits, _searchPopups);
    private IEnumerable<DocumentRow> FilteredDocumentRows => (ReportData?.DocumentHits ?? [])
        .Select(item =>
        {
            var ext = Path.GetExtension(item.Key).ToLowerInvariant();
            var avgMs = ReportData?.DocumentAvgTime.GetValueOrDefault(item.Key) ?? 0;
            return new DocumentRow(
                item.Key,
                string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(ext) ? "unknown" : ext.TrimStart('.'),
                item.Value.ToString("N0"),
                $"{avgMs:N0} ms");
        })
        .Where(item => FilterCore($"{item.File} {item.TypeLabel}", _searchDocs))
        .OrderByDescending(item => int.Parse(item.DownloadsLabel.Replace(",", string.Empty)));

    private IEnumerable<StatusRow> FilteredStatusRows => (ReportData?.StatusCodes ?? [])
        .OrderByDescending(item => item.Value)
        .Select(item => new StatusRow(item.Key, IISLogViewer.Services.LogParserService.GetStatusDisplay(item.Key), item.Value.ToString("N0")))
        .Where(item => FilterCore(item.StatusDisplay, _searchStatus));

    private IEnumerable<SlowPageRow> FilteredSlowPageRows => (ReportData?.SlowPages ?? [])
        .Select(item => new SlowPageRow(item.Key, $"{item.Value:N0} ms"))
        .Where(item => FilterCore(item.Page, _searchSlow))
        .OrderByDescending(item => ParseMetric(item.AvgTimeLabel));

    private IEnumerable<HourRow> FilteredHourRows => (ReportData?.HourlyHits ?? [])
        .OrderByDescending(item => item.Value)
        .Select(item => new HourRow(item.Key.ToString("D2"), item.Value.ToString("N0")))
        .Where(item => FilterCore(item.HourLabel, _searchHours));

    private IEnumerable<UserRow> FilteredUserRows => (ReportData?.UserHits ?? [])
        .Select(item => BuildUserRow(item.Key, item.Value))
        .Where(item => FilterCore($"{item.UserName} {item.DisplayName} {item.Department} {item.Email}", _searchUsers));

    private IEnumerable<WeekdayListRow> WeekdayRows => BuildWeekdayRows();

    private void OnDocsSearchChanged(string value)
    {
        _searchDocs = value ?? "";
    }

    private void OnStatusSearchChanged(string value)
    {
        _searchStatus = value ?? "";
    }

    private void OnSlowSearchChanged(string value)
    {
        _searchSlow = value ?? "";
    }

    private void OnHoursSearchChanged(string value)
    {
        _searchHours = value ?? "";
    }

    private void OnUsersSearchChanged(string value)
    {
        _searchUsers = value ?? "";
    }

    private bool FilterCore(string search, string searchStr)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(searchStr))
            return true;
        return search.Contains(searchStr, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> FilterLabelValueRows(IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>>? source, string searchText) =>
        (source ?? [])
            .Where(item => FilterCore(item.Key, searchText))
            .OrderByDescending(item => item.Value)
            .Select(item => new LabelValueRow(item.Key, item.Value.ToString("N0")));

    private IEnumerable<TopPageInsightRow> BuildTopPageInsights()
    {
        var pageHits = ReportData?.PageHits ?? new Dictionary<string, int>();
        var entryHits = ReportData?.PageEntryHits ?? new Dictionary<string, int>();
        var transitions = ReportData?.PageNextPageHits ?? new Dictionary<string, Dictionary<string, int>>();

        foreach (var page in pageHits.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            var entries = entryHits.TryGetValue(page.Key, out var entryCount) ? entryCount : 0;

            var topNext = "-";
            var hasFlow = false;
            if (transitions.TryGetValue(page.Key, out var nextMap) && nextMap.Any())
            {
                var next = nextMap
                    .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
                    .ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                    .First();
                topNext = $"{next.Key} ({next.Value:N0})";
                hasFlow = true;
            }

            yield return new TopPageInsightRow(
                page.Key,
                page.Value.ToString("N0"),
                entries.ToString("N0"),
                topNext,
                hasFlow);
        }
    }

    private IEnumerable<NextPageFlowRow> SelectedNextPageFlowRows =>
        BuildNextPageFlowRows(_selectedFlowPage).Take(5);

    private IEnumerable<NextPageFlowRow> BuildNextPageFlowRows(string page)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(page))
            yield break;

        var transitions = ReportData?.PageNextPageHits ?? new Dictionary<string, Dictionary<string, int>>();
        if (!transitions.TryGetValue(page, out var nextMap) || !nextMap.Any())
            yield break;

        foreach (var item in nextMap.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            yield return new NextPageFlowRow(item.Key, item.Value.ToString("N0"));
        }
    }

    private static int ParseMetric(string value) =>
        int.TryParse(value.Replace(" ms", string.Empty).Replace(",", string.Empty), out var parsed) ? parsed : 0;

    private sealed record DocumentRow(string File, string TypeLabel, string DownloadsLabel, string AvgTimeLabel);
    private sealed record StatusRow(int StatusCode, string StatusDisplay, string CountLabel);
    private sealed record SlowPageRow(string Page, string AvgTimeLabel);
    private sealed record HourRow(string HourLabel, string HitsLabel);
    private sealed record WeekdayListRow(int DayIndex, string DayLabel, string HitsLabel);
    private sealed record TopPageInsightRow(string Page, string HitsLabel, string EntryHitsLabel, string TopNextPage, bool HasFlowDetails);
    private sealed record NextPageFlowRow(string NextPage, string CountLabel);
    private sealed record UserRow(string UserName, string DisplayName, string Department, string Email, string HitsLabel);

    private int _pageSize = 10;

    private string _docSortField = nameof(DocumentRow.DownloadsLabel);
    private bool _docSortDesc = true;

    private string _statusSortField = nameof(StatusRow.CountLabel);
    private bool _statusSortDesc = true;

    private string _slowSortField = nameof(SlowPageRow.AvgTimeLabel);
    private bool _slowSortDesc = true;

    private string _hourSortField = nameof(HourRow.HitsLabel);
    private bool _hourSortDesc = true;

    private string _userSortField = nameof(UserRow.HitsLabel);
    private bool _userSortDesc = true;

    private bool _showHourlyDetailsPopup;
    private int _selectedHour;
    private bool _showWeekdayDetailsPopup;
    private int _selectedWeekday;
    private bool _showUserDetailsPopup;
    private string _selectedUser = "";
    private string _selectedUserDisplayName = "";
    private bool _showNextPageFlowPopup;
    private string _selectedFlowPage = "";

    private static int ParseNumber(string formatted) =>
        int.TryParse(formatted.Replace(",", string.Empty), out var parsed) ? parsed : 0;

    private IEnumerable<DocumentRow> SortDocuments(IEnumerable<DocumentRow> rows, string sortField, bool desc)
    {
        Func<DocumentRow, object> keySelector = sortField switch
        {
            nameof(DocumentRow.File) => r => r.File,
            nameof(DocumentRow.TypeLabel) => r => r.TypeLabel,
            nameof(DocumentRow.AvgTimeLabel) => r => ParseMetric(r.AvgTimeLabel),
            _ => r => ParseNumber(r.DownloadsLabel)
        };
        return desc ? rows.OrderByDescending(keySelector) : rows.OrderBy(keySelector);
    }

    private IEnumerable<StatusRow> SortStatus(IEnumerable<StatusRow> rows, string sortField, bool desc)
    {
        Func<StatusRow, object> keySelector = sortField switch
        {
            nameof(StatusRow.StatusDisplay) => r => r.StatusCode,
            _ => r => ParseNumber(r.CountLabel)
        };
        return desc ? rows.OrderByDescending(keySelector) : rows.OrderBy(keySelector);
    }

    private IEnumerable<SlowPageRow> SortSlow(IEnumerable<SlowPageRow> rows, string sortField, bool desc)
    {
        Func<SlowPageRow, object> keySelector = sortField switch
        {
            nameof(SlowPageRow.Page) => r => r.Page,
            _ => r => ParseMetric(r.AvgTimeLabel)
        };
        return desc ? rows.OrderByDescending(keySelector) : rows.OrderBy(keySelector);
    }

    private IEnumerable<HourRow> SortHours(IEnumerable<HourRow> rows, string sortField, bool desc)
    {
        Func<HourRow, object> keySelector = sortField switch
        {
            nameof(HourRow.HourLabel) => r => ParseNumber(r.HourLabel),
            _ => r => ParseNumber(r.HitsLabel)
        };
        return desc ? rows.OrderByDescending(keySelector) : rows.OrderBy(keySelector);
    }

    private IEnumerable<UserRow> SortUsers(IEnumerable<UserRow> rows, string sortField, bool desc)
    {
        Func<UserRow, object> keySelector = sortField switch
        {
            nameof(UserRow.UserName) => r => r.UserName,
            nameof(UserRow.DisplayName) => r => r.DisplayName,
            nameof(UserRow.Department) => r => r.Department,
            _ => r => ParseNumber(r.HitsLabel)
        };
        return desc ? rows.OrderByDescending(keySelector) : rows.OrderBy(keySelector);
    }

    private static string SortGlyph(string activeField, bool desc, string field) =>
        activeField == field ? (desc ? "▼" : "▲") : "";

    private List<DocumentRow> SortedDocuments =>
        SortDocuments(FilteredDocumentRows, _docSortField, _docSortDesc).ToList();

    private void ToggleDocSort(string field) => ToggleSort(ref _docSortField, ref _docSortDesc, field);

    private List<StatusRow> SortedStatuses =>
        SortStatus(FilteredStatusRows, _statusSortField, _statusSortDesc).ToList();

    private void ToggleStatusSort(string field) => ToggleSort(ref _statusSortField, ref _statusSortDesc, field);

    private List<SlowPageRow> SortedSlowPages =>
        SortSlow(FilteredSlowPageRows, _slowSortField, _slowSortDesc).ToList();

    private void ToggleSlowSort(string field) => ToggleSort(ref _slowSortField, ref _slowSortDesc, field);

    private List<HourRow> SortedHours =>
        SortHours(FilteredHourRows, _hourSortField, _hourSortDesc).ToList();

    private void ToggleHourSort(string field) => ToggleSort(ref _hourSortField, ref _hourSortDesc, field);

    private List<UserRow> SortedUsers =>
        SortUsers(FilteredUserRows, _userSortField, _userSortDesc).ToList();

    private void ToggleUserSort(string field) => ToggleSort(ref _userSortField, ref _userSortDesc, field);

    private static void ToggleSort(ref string sortField, ref bool sortDesc, string field)
    {
        if (sortField == field)
        {
            sortDesc = !sortDesc;
            return;
        }

        sortField = field;
        sortDesc = true;
    }

    private void OpenHourlyPopup(string hourLabel)
    {
        if (!int.TryParse(hourLabel, out var parsedHour))
            return;

        _selectedHour = parsedHour;
        _showHourlyDetailsPopup = true;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void CloseHourlyPopup()
    {
        _showHourlyDetailsPopup = false;
    }

    private void OpenWeekdayPopup(int dayIndex)
    {
        if (dayIndex is < 0 or > 6)
            return;

        _selectedWeekday = dayIndex;
        _showWeekdayDetailsPopup = true;
    }

    private void CloseWeekdayPopup()
    {
        _showWeekdayDetailsPopup = false;
    }

    private void OpenUserPopup(string userName)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(userName))
            return;

        _selectedUser = userName;
        _selectedUserDisplayName = LogParserService.GetUserDisplayName(userName);
        _showUserDetailsPopup = true;
    }

    private void CloseUserPopup()
    {
        _showUserDetailsPopup = false;
    }

    private void OpenNextPageFlowPopup(string page)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(page))
            return;

        _selectedFlowPage = page;
        _showNextPageFlowPopup = true;
    }

    private void CloseNextPageFlowPopup()
    {
        _showNextPageFlowPopup = false;
        _selectedFlowPage = "";
    }

    private void CloseAllPopups()
    {
        _showHourlyDetailsPopup = false;
        _showWeekdayDetailsPopup = false;
        _showUserDetailsPopup = false;
        CloseNextPageFlowPopup();
    }

    private UserRow BuildUserRow(string userName, int hits)
    {
        var profile = LogParserService.GetUserProfile(userName);
        return new UserRow(
            userName,
            profile?.Name ?? userName,
            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(profile?.Department) ? "Unknown" : profile!.Department,
            profile?.Email ?? "",
            hits.ToString("N0"));
    }

    private IEnumerable<WeekdayListRow> BuildWeekdayRows()
    {
        var source = ReportData?.WeekdayHits ?? new Dictionary<int, int>();
        var order = new[]
        {
            DayOfWeek.Monday,
            DayOfWeek.Tuesday,
            DayOfWeek.Wednesday,
            DayOfWeek.Thursday,
            DayOfWeek.Friday,
            DayOfWeek.Saturday,
            DayOfWeek.Sunday
        };

        foreach (var day in order)
        {
            var key = (int)day;
            var hits = source.TryGetValue(key, out var count) ? count : 0;
            yield return new WeekdayListRow(key, day.ToString(), hits.ToString("N0"));
        }
    }
}

FILE: Components/Pages/ReportSelected.razor
------------------------------------------------------------
@page "/report"
@rendermode InteractiveServer
@inject IISLogViewer.Services.LogParserService LogParser
@inject IISLogViewer.Services.SelectionState SelectionState
@implements IDisposable

<div class="page-header">
    <h5>@ReportTitle</h5>
</div>

@if (!SelectionState.SelectedDays.Any())
{
    <div class="info-banner">
        Select dates from the tree on the left to generate a report.
    </div>
}
else if (_isLoading)
{
    <div class="loading-state">
        <TelerikLoader Size="@ThemeConstants.Loader.Size.Medium" Type="@LoaderType.InfiniteSpinner" />
        <span>Loading report for @SelectionState.SelectedDays.Count day(s)...</span>
    </div>
}
else if (CurrentReport == null)
{
    <div class="info-banner">
        No data was returned for the selected dates.
    </div>
}
else
{
    <div class="stats-grid">
        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value">@CurrentReport.TotalHits.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Total Hits</div>
        </article>
        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value stat-card__value--success">@SuccessCount.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Successful (2xx/3xx)</div>
        </article>
        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value stat-card__value--warning">@ClientErrorCount.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Client Errors (4xx)</div>
        </article>
        <article class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-card__value stat-card__value--error">@ServerErrorCount.ToString("N0")</div>
            <div class="stat-card__label">Server Errors (5xx)</div>
        </article>
    </div>

    <section class="surface-panel">
        <Report ReportData="CurrentReport" SelectedDays="SelectionState.SelectedDays" />
    </section>
}

@code {
    private IISLogViewer.Services.LogReport? CurrentReport;
    private string ReportTitle = "Report";
    private int SuccessCount;
    private int ClientErrorCount;
    private int ServerErrorCount;
    private bool _isLoading;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        SelectionState.OnChange += OnSelectionChanged;
        await LoadReport();
    }

    private async void OnSelectionChanged()
    {
        await LoadReport();
        await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
    }

    private async Task LoadReport()
    {
        _isLoading = true;
        CurrentReport = null;
        await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);

        try
        {
            if (!SelectionState.SelectedDays.Any())
            {
                ReportTitle = "Report";
                return;
            }

            var days = SelectionState.SelectedDays.ToList();

            ReportTitle = days.Count == 1
                ? $"Report for {days[0]:dddd, dd MMMM yyyy}"
                : $"Report for {days.Count} selected days ({days.Min():dd MMM yyyy} — {days.Max():dd MMM yyyy})";

            if (days.Count == 1)
            {
                CurrentReport = await LogParser.ParseFile(days[0]);
            }
            else
            {
                CurrentReport = await LogParser.ParseDates(days);
            }

            if (CurrentReport != null)
            {
                SuccessCount = CurrentReport.StatusCodes
                    .Where(s => s.Key >= 200 && s.Key < 400).Sum(s => s.Value);
                ClientErrorCount = CurrentReport.StatusCodes
                    .Where(s => s.Key >= 400 && s.Key < 500).Sum(s => s.Value);
                ServerErrorCount = CurrentReport.StatusCodes
                    .Where(s => s.Key >= 500).Sum(s => s.Value);
            }
        }
        finally
        {
            _isLoading = false;
            await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
        }
    }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        SelectionState.OnChange -= OnSelectionChanged;
    }
}

<PageTitle>Weather</PageTitle>

    <div class="d-flex align-items-center gap-2">

            <GridColumn Field="@nameof(WeatherForecast.Date)" Title="Date">
                <Template Context="itemObj">
                    @{ var forecast = (WeatherForecast)itemObj; }
                    @forecast.Date.ToShortDateString()
                </Template>
            </GridColumn>
            <GridColumn Field="@nameof(WeatherForecast.TemperatureC)" Title="Temp. (C)" />
            <GridColumn Field="@nameof(WeatherForecast.TemperatureF)" Title="Temp. (F)" />

@code {
    private WeatherForecast[]? forecasts;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        // Simulate asynchronous loading to demonstrate streaming rendering
        await Task.Delay(500);

        var startDate = DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Now);
        var summaries = new[] { "Freezing", "Bracing", "Chilly", "Cool", "Mild", "Warm", "Balmy", "Hot", "Sweltering", "Scorching" };
        forecasts = Enumerable.Range(1, 5).Select(index => new WeatherForecast
        {
            Date = startDate.AddDays(index),
            TemperatureC = Random.Shared.Next(-20, 55),
            Summary = summaries[Random.Shared.Next(summaries.Length)]
        }).ToArray();
    }

    private class WeatherForecast
    {
        public DateOnly Date { get; set; }
        public int TemperatureC { get; set; }
        public string? Summary { get; set; }
        public int TemperatureF => 32 + (int)(TemperatureC / 0.5556);
    }
}

@code {
    private int _pageSize = 10;
    [Parameter]
    public bool IsOpen { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public int SelectedHour { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public IISLogViewer.Services.LogReport? ReportData { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public EventCallback OnClose { get; set; }

    private const int MaxRows = 12;

    private string SelectedHourLabel => SelectedHour.ToString("D2");

    private List<ItemHitRow> TopPagesRows => MapRows(GetTopByHour(ReportData?.HourlyPageHits, SelectedHour));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopDocumentsRows => MapRows(GetTopByHour(ReportData?.HourlyDocumentHits, SelectedHour));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopPopupsRows => MapRows(GetTopByHour(ReportData?.HourlyPopupHits, SelectedHour));

    private static IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>> GetTopByHour(
        Dictionary<int, Dictionary<string, int>>? source,
        int hour)
    {
        if (source == null || !source.TryGetValue(hour, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return Enumerable.Empty<KeyValuePair<string, int>>();

        return bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(MaxRows);
    }

    private static List<ItemHitRow> MapRows(IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>> source) =>
        source.Select(x => new ItemHitRow(x.Key, x.Value)).ToList();

    private Task Close() => OnClose.InvokeAsync();

    private sealed record ItemHitRow(string Item, int Hits);
}

public sealed record LabelValueRow(string Label, string ValueLabel);


FILE: Components/Shared/LabelValueSection.razor
------------------------------------------------------------
@namespace IISLogViewer.Components.Shared

<div class="grid-toolbar">
    <div><h3>@Title</h3></div>
    <TelerikTextBox Value="@SearchValue"
                    ValueChanged="OnSearchValueChanged"
                    Placeholder="@Placeholder"
                    Width="260px"
                    Size="@ThemeConstants.TextBox.Size.Small"
                    FillMode="@ThemeConstants.TextBox.FillMode.Outline"
                    DebounceDelay="250"
                    ShowClearButton="true" />
</div>

@if (!Rows.Any())
{
    <div class="empty-state">No data found.</div>
}
else
{
    <TelerikGrid Data="@SortedRows"
                 Pageable="true"
                 @bind-PageSize="_pageSize"
                 Sortable="false"
                 Resizable="true"
                 Size="@ThemeConstants.Grid.Size.Small">
        <GridColumns>
            <GridColumn Field="@nameof(LabelValueRow.Label)" Title="@LabelHeader">
                <HeaderTemplate>
                    <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ToggleSort(nameof(LabelValueRow.Label))"
                                   FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Flat"
                                   Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small">
                        @LabelHeader @SortGlyph(nameof(LabelValueRow.Label))
                    </TelerikButton>
                </HeaderTemplate>
            </GridColumn>
            <GridColumn Field="@nameof(LabelValueRow.ValueLabel)" Title="@ValueHeader" Width="140px">
                <HeaderTemplate>
                    <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ToggleSort(nameof(LabelValueRow.ValueLabel))"
                                   FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Flat"
                                   Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small">
                        @ValueHeader @SortGlyph(nameof(LabelValueRow.ValueLabel))
                    </TelerikButton>
                </HeaderTemplate>
                <Template Context="itemObj">
                    @{ var row = (LabelValueRow)itemObj; }
                    <div class="text-start">@row.ValueLabel</div>
                </Template>
            </GridColumn>
        </GridColumns>
    </TelerikGrid>
}

@code {
    [Parameter] public string Title { get; set; } = "";
    [Parameter] public string Placeholder { get; set; } = "";
    [Parameter] public string LabelHeader { get; set; } = "Label";
    [Parameter] public string ValueHeader { get; set; } = "Hits";

    [Parameter] public string SearchValue { get; set; } = "";
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<string> SearchValueChanged { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> Rows { get; set; } = Array.Empty<LabelValueRow>();

    private int _pageSize = 10;

    private string _sortField = nameof(LabelValueRow.ValueLabel);
    private bool _sortDesc = true;

    private IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> SortedRows =>
        Sort(Rows, _sortField, _sortDesc);

    private async Task OnSearchValueChanged(string value)
    {
        await SearchValueChanged.InvokeAsync(value ?? "");
    }

    private void ToggleSort(string field)
    {
        if (_sortField == field)
        {
            _sortDesc = !_sortDesc;
            return;
        }

        _sortField = field;
        _sortDesc = true;
    }

    private string SortGlyph(string field) =>
        _sortField == field ? (_sortDesc ? "▼" : "▲") : "";

    private static IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> Sort(IEnumerable<LabelValueRow> rows, string field, bool desc)
    {
        Func<LabelValueRow, object> key = field switch
        {
            nameof(LabelValueRow.Label) => r => r.Label,
            _ => r => ParseNumber(r.ValueLabel)
        };
        return desc ? rows.OrderByDescending(key) : rows.OrderBy(key);
    }

    private static int ParseNumber(string formatted) =>
        int.TryParse(formatted.Replace(",", string.Empty), out var parsed) ? parsed : 0;

}

FILE: Components/Shared/Pager.razor
------------------------------------------------------------
@namespace IISLogViewer.Components.Shared

@if (TotalPages > 1)
{
    <div class="d-flex align-items-center justify-content-between mt-2">
        <small class="text-muted">Page @CurrentPage of @TotalPages</small>
        <div class="d-flex gap-2">
            <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ChangeTo(CurrentPage - 1)"
                           Enabled="@(CurrentPage > 1)"
                           Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small"
                           FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Outline">
                Prev
            </TelerikButton>
            <TelerikButton OnClick="() => ChangeTo(CurrentPage + 1)"
                           Enabled="@(CurrentPage < TotalPages)"
                           Size="@ThemeConstants.Button.Size.Small"
                           FillMode="@ThemeConstants.Button.FillMode.Outline">
                Next
            </TelerikButton>
        </div>
    </div>
}

@code {
    [Parameter] public int CurrentPage { get; set; } = 1;
    [Parameter] public int TotalPages { get; set; } = 1;
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<int> OnPageChanged { get; set; }

    private async Task ChangeTo(int nextPage)
    {
        var page = Math.Clamp(nextPage, 1, Math.Max(1, TotalPages));
        if (page == CurrentPage)
            return;
        await OnPageChanged.InvokeAsync(page);
    }
}

                                    <GridColumn Field="@nameof(UserTimelineRow.EventType)" Title="Type" Width="100px" />

                                    <GridColumn Field="@nameof(UserTimelineRow.DurationLabel)" Title="Duration" Width="120px" />
                                </GridColumns>
                            </TelerikGrid>
                        </div>
                    }
                </TabStripTab>
            </TelerikTabStrip>

        </WindowContent>
    </TelerikWindow>
}

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public bool IsOpen { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public string SelectedUser { get; set; } = "";

    [Parameter]
    public string SelectedUserDisplayName { get; set; } = "";

    [Parameter]
    public IEnumerable<DateTime>? SelectedDays { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public IISLogViewer.Services.LogReport? ReportData { get; set; }

    [Inject]
    public IISLogViewer.Services.LogParserService LogParserService { get; set; } = default!;

    [Parameter]
    public EventCallback OnClose { get; set; }

    private string _timelineUserSeed = "";
    private string _timelineSelectionSeed = "";
    private string _selectedTimelineDateKey = "";
    private List<TimelineDateOption> _timelineDateOptions = new();
    private List<UserTimelineRow> _timelineRows = new();
    private bool _timelineLoading;
    private int _gridPageSize = 10;

    private const int MaxRows = 12;

    private IISLogViewer.Services.UserProfile? SelectedProfile =>
        string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(SelectedUser) ? null : LogParserService.GetUserProfile(SelectedUser);

    private string HeaderDisplayName =>
        string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(SelectedUserDisplayName) ? SelectedUser : SelectedUserDisplayName;

    private string HeaderSubTitle
    {
        get
        {
            var parts = new List<string> { SelectedUser };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(SelectedProfile?.Department))
                parts.Add(SelectedProfile.Department);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(SelectedProfile?.Email))
                parts.Add(SelectedProfile.Email);
            return string.Join(" | ", parts.Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x)));
        }
    }

    private List<ItemHitRow> TopPagesRows => MapRows(GetTopByUser(ReportData?.UserPageHits, SelectedUser));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopDocumentsRows => MapRows(GetTopByUser(ReportData?.UserDocumentHits, SelectedUser));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopPopupsRows => MapRows(GetTopByUser(ReportData?.UserPopupHits, SelectedUser));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopStatusRows => GetTopStatusByUser(ReportData?.UserStatusHits, SelectedUser)
        .Select(item => new ItemHitRow(IISLogViewer.Services.LogParserService.GetStatusDisplay(item.Key), item.Value))
        .ToList();
    private List<HourHitRow> TopHoursRows => GetTopHoursByUser(ReportData?.UserHourlyHits, SelectedUser)
        .Select(item => new HourHitRow($"{item.Key:D2}:00-{item.Key:D2}:59", item.Value))
        .ToList();

    private PeakHourInfo? PeakHourSummary => BuildPeakHour(ReportData?.UserHourlyHits, SelectedUser, SelectedUserTotalHits);

    private int SelectedUserTotalHits => ReportData?.UserHits.TryGetValue(SelectedUser, out var hits) == true ? hits : 0;

    private List<WeekdayRow> WeekdayRows => BuildWeekdayRows(ReportData?.UserWeekdayHits, SelectedUser, SelectedUserTotalHits).ToList();

    protected override async Task OnParametersSetAsync()
    {
        var currentSelectionSeed = BuildSelectionSeed(SelectedDays);

        if (!IsOpen || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(SelectedUser))
        {
            _timelineUserSeed = "";
            _timelineSelectionSeed = "";
            _selectedTimelineDateKey = "";
            _timelineDateOptions = new List<TimelineDateOption>();
            _timelineRows = new List<UserTimelineRow>();
            return;
        }

        if (string.Equals(_timelineUserSeed, SelectedUser, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
            string.Equals(_timelineSelectionSeed, currentSelectionSeed, StringComparison.Ordinal) &&
            _timelineDateOptions.Count > 0)
            return;

        _timelineUserSeed = SelectedUser;
        _timelineSelectionSeed = currentSelectionSeed;
        await RefreshTimelineDatesAsync();
    }

    private async Task RefreshTimelineDatesAsync()
    {
        var dates = await LogParserService.GetTimelineDatesForUser(SelectedUser);

        var selectedDaySet = SelectedDays?
            .Select(d => d.Date)
            .ToHashSet() ?? new HashSet<DateTime>();

        if (selectedDaySet.Count > 0)
            dates = dates.Where(d => selectedDaySet.Contains(d.Date)).ToList();

        _timelineDateOptions = dates
            .Select(d => new TimelineDateOption(d.ToString("dd MMM yyyy"), d.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")))
            .ToList();

        _selectedTimelineDateKey = _timelineDateOptions.FirstOrDefault()?.Value ?? string.Empty;
        await LoadTimelineAsync();
    }

    private async Task OnTimelineDateChanged(string value)
    {
        _selectedTimelineDateKey = value ?? string.Empty;
        await LoadTimelineAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadTimelineAsync()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(SelectedUser) ||
            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_selectedTimelineDateKey) ||
            !DateTime.TryParse(_selectedTimelineDateKey, out var selectedDate))
        {
            _timelineRows = new List<UserTimelineRow>();
            return;
        }

        _timelineLoading = true;
        try
        {
            var events = await LogParserService.ParseTimelineDayForUser(selectedDate.Date, SelectedUser);
            _timelineRows = events
                .OrderBy(e => e.TimestampLocal)
                .Select(e => new UserTimelineRow(
                    e.TimestampLocal.ToString("HH:mm:ss"),
                    e.Action,
                    e.EventType,
                    e.StatusCode > 0 ? e.StatusCode.ToString() : "-",
                    e.DurationMs > 0 ? $"{e.DurationMs:N0} ms" : "-"))
                .ToList();
        }
        finally
        {
            _timelineLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private static IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>> GetTopByUser(
        Dictionary<string, Dictionary<string, int>>? source,
        string user)
    {
        if (source == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(user) || !source.TryGetValue(user, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return Enumerable.Empty<KeyValuePair<string, int>>();

        return bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(MaxRows);
    }

    private static IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<int, int>> GetTopStatusByUser(
        Dictionary<string, Dictionary<int, int>>? source,
        string user)
    {
        if (source == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(user) || !source.TryGetValue(user, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return Enumerable.Empty<KeyValuePair<int, int>>();

        return bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key)
            .Take(MaxRows);
    }

    private static IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<int, int>> GetTopHoursByUser(
        Dictionary<string, Dictionary<int, int>>? source,
        string user)
    {
        if (source == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(user) || !source.TryGetValue(user, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return Enumerable.Empty<KeyValuePair<int, int>>();

        return bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key)
            .Take(MaxRows);
    }

    private static PeakHourInfo? BuildPeakHour(
        Dictionary<string, Dictionary<int, int>>? source,
        string user,
        int totalHits)
    {
        if (totalHits <= 0)
            return null;

        if (source == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(user) || !source.TryGetValue(user, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return null;

        var peak = bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.Key)
            .First();

        if (peak.Value <= 0)
            return null;

        var percent = (peak.Value * 100.0) / totalHits;
        return new PeakHourInfo($"{peak.Key:D2}:00-{peak.Key:D2}:59", peak.Value, $"{percent:F1}% of user traffic");
    }

    private static IEnumerable<WeekdayRow> BuildWeekdayRows(
        Dictionary<string, Dictionary<int, int>>? source,
        string user,
        int totalHits)
    {
        var weekdayOrder = new[]
        {
            DayOfWeek.Monday,
            DayOfWeek.Tuesday,
            DayOfWeek.Wednesday,
            DayOfWeek.Thursday,
            DayOfWeek.Friday,
            DayOfWeek.Saturday,
            DayOfWeek.Sunday
        };

        var bucket = (source != null && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(user) && source.TryGetValue(user, out var found))
            ? found
            : new Dictionary<int, int>();

        foreach (var day in weekdayOrder)
        {
            var key = (int)day;
            var hits = bucket.TryGetValue(key, out var value) ? value : 0;
            var pct = totalHits > 0 ? (hits * 100.0) / totalHits : 0;
            yield return new WeekdayRow(day.ToString()[..3], hits.ToString("N0"), $"{pct:F1}%");
        }
    }

    private static List<ItemHitRow> MapRows(IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>> source) =>
        source.Select(x => new ItemHitRow(x.Key, x.Value)).ToList();

    private static string BuildSelectionSeed(IEnumerable<DateTime>? selectedDays)
    {
        if (selectedDays == null)
            return string.Empty;

        return string.Join("|", selectedDays
            .Select(d => d.Date)
            .Distinct()
            .OrderBy(d => d)
            .Select(d => d.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")));
    }

    private Task Close() => OnClose.InvokeAsync();

    private sealed record ItemHitRow(string Item, int Hits);
    private sealed record HourHitRow(string HourLabel, int Hits);
    private sealed record PeakHourInfo(string HourLabel, int Hits, string PercentageLabel);
    private sealed record WeekdayRow(string DayLabel, string HitsLabel, string PercentLabel);
    private sealed record TimelineDateOption(string Text, string Value);
    private sealed record UserTimelineRow(string TimeLabel, string Action, string EventType, string StatusLabel, string DurationLabel);
}

@code {
    private int _pageSize = 10;
    [Parameter]
    public bool IsOpen { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public int SelectedWeekday { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public IISLogViewer.Services.LogReport? ReportData { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    public EventCallback OnClose { get; set; }

    private const int MaxRows = 12;

    private string SelectedWeekdayLabel => DayLabel(SelectedWeekday);

    private List<ItemHitRow> TopPagesRows => MapRows(GetTopByWeekday(ReportData?.WeekdayPageHits, SelectedWeekday));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopPopupsRows => MapRows(GetTopByWeekday(ReportData?.WeekdayPopupHits, SelectedWeekday));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopDocumentsRows => MapRows(GetTopByWeekday(ReportData?.WeekdayDocumentHits, SelectedWeekday));
    private List<ItemHitRow> TopUsersRows => MapRows(GetTopUsersByWeekday(ReportData?.WeekdayUserHits, SelectedWeekday));
    private List<HourHitRow> TopHoursRows => GetTopHoursByWeekday(ReportData?.WeekdayHourHits, SelectedWeekday)
        .Select(x => new HourHitRow($"{x.Key:D2}:00-{x.Key:D2}:59", x.Value))
        .ToList();

    private static IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>> GetTopByWeekday(
        Dictionary<int, Dictionary<string, int>>? source,
        int weekday)
    {
        if (source == null || !source.TryGetValue(weekday, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return Enumerable.Empty<KeyValuePair<string, int>>();

        return bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(MaxRows);
    }

    private IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>> GetTopUsersByWeekday(
        Dictionary<int, Dictionary<string, int>>? source,
        int weekday)
    {
        if (source == null || !source.TryGetValue(weekday, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return Enumerable.Empty<KeyValuePair<string, int>>();

        return bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(MaxRows)
            .Select(item =>
            {
                var displayName = LogParserService.GetUserDisplayName(item.Key);
                var label = string.Equals(displayName, item.Key, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                    ? item.Key
                    : $"{displayName} ({item.Key})";
                return new KeyValuePair<string, int>(label, item.Value);
            });
    }

    private static IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<int, int>> GetTopHoursByWeekday(
        Dictionary<int, Dictionary<int, int>>? source,
        int weekday)
    {
        if (source == null || !source.TryGetValue(weekday, out var bucket) || bucket.Count == 0)
            return Enumerable.Empty<KeyValuePair<int, int>>();

        return bucket
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key)
            .Take(MaxRows);
    }

    private static string DayLabel(int dayIndex)
    {
        if (dayIndex is < 0 or > 6)
            return $"Day {dayIndex}";

        return ((DayOfWeek)dayIndex).ToString();
    }

    private static List<ItemHitRow> MapRows(IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<string, int>> source) =>
        source.Select(x => new ItemHitRow(x.Key, x.Value)).ToList();

    private Task Close() => OnClose.InvokeAsync();

    private sealed record ItemHitRow(string Item, int Hits);
    private sealed record HourHitRow(string HourLabel, int Hits);
}

FILE: Program.cs
------------------------------------------------------------
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Web;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

builder.Services.AddRazorComponents()
    .AddInteractiveServerComponents();

builder.Services.AddTelerikBlazor();
builder.Services.AddScoped<IISLogViewer.Services.SelectionState>();

var logRoot = builder.Configuration["LogViewer:RootDirectory"];
var timeZoneId = builder.Configuration["LogViewer:TimeZoneId"];
var userCsvPath = builder.Configuration["LogViewer:UserCsvPath"];
if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(logRoot))
{
    logRoot = Path.Combine(Directory.GetCurrentDirectory(), "LogFiles");
}

builder.Services.AddScoped(_ => new IISLogViewer.Services.LogParserService(logRoot, timeZoneId, userCsvPath));

var app = builder.Build();

if (!app.Environment.IsDevelopment())
{
    app.UseExceptionHandler("/Error");
    app.UseHsts();
}

app.UseHttpsRedirection();
app.UseStaticFiles();
app.UseAntiforgery();

app.MapRazorComponents<IISLogViewer.Components.App>()
    .AddInteractiveServerRenderMode();

app.Run();
